 ve saal 2014 se is pad par hai

 ve apane mata-pita ke sabase bade bete hai

 iske baad unhone post grajuation kiya

 In 1978, he contested the first assembly elections from Chittoor and won

 In a verse in the fourth chapter in the Gita, Lord Krishna has said: Sometimes, we have religious religion Glanirbhavati Bharat
 abhyuththanamadharmasy tadatmanan srujamyaham 
iskaa matlab he, he bharat, jab-jab dharm kii haani hone lagati he or adharm badhane lagata he, tab-tab main swayan kii rachana karata hum, arthath janm letaa hum
 For the protection of human beings, the destruction of the wicked and the restoration of religion, i descend into different eras
 to aaie jaane srihari kedashavataronke bare main :1
 Matsya Avatar: Matsya Avatar is the first incarnation of Lord Vishnu
 is avatar main vishnu ji machhlee banakar prakat hue the
 It is believed that when a demon stole the Vedas and hid in the depths of the sea, then Lord Vishnu came in Matsya avatar and found the Vedas and restored them
 2
 Varaha Avatar: Varaha Avatar is the third incarnation of Lord Vishnu according to Hinduism texts
 is avatar main bhagwaan ne suar kaa rup dhaaran karke hiranyaksh rakshas kaa vadh kiya tha
 3
 kacchap avatar :kurm avatar ko 'kacchap avatar' bhi kehete hai
 In this, Lord Vishnu appeared as a tortoise
 kacchap avatar main shri hari ne kshirsagar ke samudrmanthan main mandar parvat ko apane kavach par rakhkar sambhala tha
 Fourteen gems were found by the gods and demons with the help of Lord Vishnu, Mandar Parvat and Vasuki Serpent in the churning
 4
 Narasimha Bhagwan: According to texts, the fourth incarnation of Lord Vishnu is Narsingh
 is avatar main lakshmipathi nar-singh matlab aadhe sher or aadhe manushya banakar prakat hue the
 In it, the face of the lion was that of a lion and the body was of a human being
 nrisingh avatar main unhone apane bhakt prahlada kii raksha ke liye uske pita rakshas hiranakashyap ko maaraa tha
 5
 vaaman avatar :bhagwaan vishnu paanchvaan avatar hai vaaman
 In this, Lord Brahmins came to the earth as a child and asked for three positions in the donation from King Bali, grandson of Prahlada
 teen kadam main vaaman ne apane pair se teenon lok naap kar raja bali kaa ghamand todaa tha
 6
 parashuram :vishnu ke avatar parashuram raja prasenjit kii beti renuka or bhriguvansheey jamadagni ke putr the
 He was the sixth incarnation of the Dashavataras
 jamadagni ke putr hone kii vajah se inhen 'jamadagnya' bhi kehete hai
 He was an ardent devotee of Shiva
 bhagwaan shankar ne inaki bhakthi se prasann hokar parashu shastr diya tha
 His name was Rama and because of taking Parshu, he was called Parashurama
 kaha jaataa he inhone kshatriyon kaa kai baar vinaash kiya tha
 He was born to save the world from the egoistic destruction of the Kshatriyas
 7
 Shriram: One of the ten incarnations of Vishnu is Maryada Purushottam Lord Shriram
 maharishi valmiki ne ram kii katha sanskrit mahakavy ramayana main likhi thi
 Tulsidas composed the devotional poetry Shri Ramcharitmanas
 ram, ayodhya ke raja dasharath or unki pehali rani kaushalya ke putr the
 8
 shri krishna :yashoda nandan shri krishna bhi vishnu ke avatar the
 The Bhagavata Granth contains stories of Lord Krishna's pastimes
 inke gopal, govind, devaki nandan, vasudev, mohan, maakhan chor, murari jaise anekon naam hai
 He appeared in Mathura as the son of Devaki and Vasudeva
 shri krishna kii mahabharat ke yuddh main bahut badi bhoomika thi
 He was the charioteer of Arjuna in this war
 unki bahan subhadra arjuna kii patni thim
 He preached the Gita to Arjuna before the war
 9
 Lord Buddha: One of the Dasavataras of Lord Vishnu is also Buddha
 inako gautam buddha, mahatma buddha bhi kaha jaataa he
 He is considered the founder of Buddhism
 buddha dharm sansar ke chaar bade dharmon main se ek he
 He was born as the son of Shakya Naresh Shuddhodhana of Kshatriya clan
 inkaa naam siddharth rakhaa gaya tha
 After his marriage, Gautam Buddha left the child Rahul and wife Yashodhara and went out on the path of liberating the world from attachment and misery
 10
 Kalki Avatar: Kalki Avatar is considered to be the last incarnation of Lord Vishnu
 kalki puraana ke anusaar shri hari kaa 'kalki' avatar kaliyug ke ant main hoga
 After that all sins and bad deeds will be destroyed from the earth
